================================================================================

WHAT IS THIS FILE?
  This file contains everything an AI needs to recreate the TopoAssist project
  from scratch. It is kept in sync with every code change made to the project.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
WORKFLOW RULE: Before making ANY code change to this project, read the relevant
INSTRUCTIONS.txt sections first. After making changes, update INSTRUCTIONS.txt
immediately (the hook enforces this). If the code and INSTRUCTIONS.txt disagree,
DO NOT silently pick one ÔÇö ask the user which is correct and confirm the intended
flow before proceeding or updating docs.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 0A: SYSTEM INVARIANTS (Must hold after every operation)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These invariants represent the highest-priority contracts in the system.
When any of these are violated, visible bugs result immediately.

1. _sys_ ALWAYS AT COL 1 OF SHEET_DATA
   Ensured by: refreshSheetRowVisibility() ÔåÆ ensureDummyColumn() inserts it.
   Post-rebuild rule: refreshSheetRowVisibility() MUST run BEFORE applyCustomView().
   If order is reversed, _sys_ is missing and applyCustomView() corrupts col 1.

2. generateConfig() ALWAYS CALLED WITH ALL 5 ARGS
   Signature: generateConfig(portName, d, ipPrefs, seenPos, netSettings)
   Both callers ÔÇö getTopologyData() and getDeviceConfig() ÔÇö must pass netSettings.
   netSettings is the full settings object (13 IP family flags). Omitting it silently
   drops all protocol-family-gated commands (OSPF per-interface, IPv6, etc.).

3. TOOLTIP CONFIG == CONFIGS SHEET CONFIG (same source of truth)
   Both paths call getDeviceConfig() ÔåÆ configMap[key].full.
   getTopologyData() pre-generates via generateConfig() with globalUnderlay.
   fetchFullConfig() ÔåÆ processDeviceConfig() maps the same configMap to allNodesData.
   Any divergence means one path is bypassing getDeviceConfig().

4. processDeviceConfig() STRIPS ^\d+_ PREFIX BEFORE canonicalizeInterface()
   configMap keys are prefixed: "050_Et1", "060_Po10", "000_GLOBAL", etc.
   Must strip prefix first: portName.replace(/^\d+_/, "") ÔåÆ canonicalizeInterface()
   Without strip: "050_Et1" does not canonicalize to "Et1", allNodesData lookup fails,
   tooltip always shows "Loading..." (silent failure, no error thrown).

5. allNodesData KEYS ARE "DeviceName:PortName" (canonical, no prefix)
   Example: "SPINE1:Et1", "LEAF1:Po10" ÔÇö never "SPINE1:050_Et1".
   canonicalizeInterface() normalizes "Ethernet1" ÔåÆ "Et1", "Port-Channel10" ÔåÆ "Po10".
   All code that reads/writes allNodesData must use this format.

6. canonicalizeInterface() IS DUPLICATED ÔÇö KEEP BOTH IN SYNC
   Lives in Code.gs (server config gen) AND Sidebar-js.html (client topology render).
   Both copies carry "// DUPLICATED ÔÇö last synced: <date>" comment.
   Update the date on BOTH copies whenever either is changed.

7. configCache[deviceName].data IS THE FULL configMap
   Format: { "050_Et1": { full: "...", ... }, "000_GLOBAL": { full: "..." }, ... }
   It is NOT a per-port string. Code that reads it must key by prefixed port name.

8. allNodesData IS FULLY REPOPULATED ON EVERY render() CALL
   It is cleared at the start of render() and rebuilt from the server payload.
   Do not persist cross-render state in allNodesData ÔÇö it will be lost.

9. selectedLineId IS A RENDERING VARIABLE ÔÇö NEVER READ IN ASYNC CALLBACKS
   selectedLineId is cleared by two render-pipeline paths without hiding the strip UI:
     a. redrawLinks() ÔÇö clears selectedLineId when link.coords=null (node hidden/zoom)
     b. filterTopology() ÔÇö always clears selectedLineId on any search input change
   By the time a GAS withSuccessHandler or fetchQueue callback fires (seconds later),
   selectedLineId is often null even though the link strip is still visible.
   RULE: any async callback or click handler needing the selected link's device/port
   must use _pushLeftDev/_pushRightDev/_pushLeftPort/_pushRightPort ÔÇö set by selectLine()
   and only changed by an explicit new selection. Never use selectedLineId for this.
   selectedDeviceId is stable (not cleared by render pipeline) ÔÇö safe in async callbacks.
   Root cause of the "strip stays amber / View button gives 'select a device or link
   first'" bug: openConfigFromButton and processDeviceConfig CASE 2 both read
   selectedLineId at async time. Fixed 2026-04-28 to use _pushLeftDev/_pushRightDev.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 0B: CRITICAL CALL CHAINS (Order matters ÔÇö do not reorder)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

POST-REBUILD (rebuildSheet or syncSchemaPreservingOrder):
  rebuildSheet() stages 1ÔåÆ5
  ÔåÆ refreshSheetRowVisibility()   ÔåÉ creates _sys_ at col 1 via ensureDummyColumn()
  ÔåÆ applyCustomView()             ÔåÉ hides/shows columns; _sys_ must already exist

TOPOLOGY LOAD (getTopologyData):
  getTopologyData(forceSync)
  ÔåÆ runFullSheetCleanup()
  ÔåÆ applyGlobalFormatting()
  ÔåÆ calculateGlobalTopology()     ÔåÉ returns { mlagConfigPorts, peerLinkPorts, mlagPeerMap, globalLinkMap }
  ÔåÆ [per-port] generateConfig(pName, details, ipPrefs, seenPos, globalNetSettings)
  ÔåÆ return payload                ÔåÉ includes pre-generated config per port

CONFIG FETCH (right pane tooltip, on demand):
  fetchFullConfig(deviceName)
  ÔåÆ google.script.run.getDeviceConfig(deviceName)
  ÔåÆ processDeviceConfig(dev, res.config)
      strips ^\d+_ prefix from each key
      ÔåÆ canonicalizeInterface(shortPort)
      ÔåÆ allNodesData[dev+":"+shortPort].details.config = configMap[key].full

CONFIGS SHEET (Generate All Configs menu):
  getAllDeviceConfigs()
  ÔåÆ [per device] getDeviceConfig(dev)   ÔåÉ same function as CONFIG FETCH path
  ÔåÆ formatConfigMap(configMap)          ÔåÉ sort keys numerically, join .full with 
!

  ÔåÆ writeConfigsToSheet()

ROW VISIBILITY (show/hide rows by filter):
  refreshSheetRowVisibility()
  ÔåÆ ensureDummyColumn()                 ÔåÉ inserts _sys_ at col 1 if missing
  ÔåÆ read headers row
  ÔåÆ show/hide rows based on filter prefs (SHEET_VIEW_*)

SCHEMA SYNC (force sync button):
  syncSchemaPreservingOrder()
  ÔåÆ orphan check (warn if data exists for removed schema keys)
  ÔåÆ rebuildSheet()
  ÔåÆ [post-rebuild chain above]

CLIENT INIT (sidebar load):
  initApp()
  ÔåÆ initTheme(), initToolbarCollapse()
  ÔåÆ renderIpTypeList(), renderIntModeList(), renderSviList()
  ÔåÆ hideGlobalLoading()
  ÔåÆ loadStateFromStorage(currentViewMode)   ÔåÉ populates savedNodePositions
  ÔåÆ loadGroupRects()
  ÔåÆ try instant restore from sessionStorage
  ÔåÆ fetchData(false, true)                  ÔåÉ auto-verify, always runs
  ÔåÆ bindGlobalSearchListeners(), initLayoutObserver()
  ÔåÆ startSmartPolling()

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 0C: TERMINOLOGY (READ BEFORE EVERY CHANGE)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Two completely separate HTML dialogs open in different contexts. Never confuse them.

  "Sheet View" / "sheet view"
      File:    SheetAssistPanel.html
      Opens:   showSheetAssistPanel() ÔÇö appears as a modeless panel INSIDE the
               Google Sheet (not the sidebar topology dialog)
      Title:   "Sheet View" (490├ù420 dialog)
      Purpose: Device visibility toggles (show/hide sheet rows per device) +
               Column view selector (hide/show sheet columns)
      Filter panels: ip_type, int_mode, svi_vlan filters ÔÇö all SheetAssistPanel.html
      User terms: "sheet view", "sheet panel", "Sheet View"

  "Topology View" / "topology view"
      Files:   Sidebar.html + Sidebar-js.html + Sidebar-css.html
      Opens:   showSidebar() ÔÇö appears as the TOPOLOGY SIDEBAR (1600├ù900 dialog)
      Purpose: Visual network topology (port cards, D3 holistic graph, edit mode,
               config push, validation, device/schema managers)
      Sub-modes (currentViewMode):
        'detailed'  ÔÇö left port-card list + D3 canvas (the default)
        'holistic'  ÔÇö D3 force-graph only (circle nodes, no port cards)
        'simple'    ÔÇö same as holistic but the Dev Vis floating panel calls it
                      "Topology View" in its header
      Dev Vis panel: floating panel labeled "Topology View" inside the sidebar ÔÇö
                     its int_mode filter uses SHORT labels (l2ea, l2etÔÇª) because
                     the panel is compact; full names live in SheetAssistPanel.
      User terms: "topology view", "sidebar", "canvas"

  RULE: If the user says "sheet view" ÔåÆ SheetAssistPanel.html.
        If the user says "topology view" or "sidebar" ÔåÆ Sidebar.html / Sidebar-js.html.
        If unsure, ASK before touching code.

ÔöÇÔöÇ VIEW TAXONOMY ÔÇö THREE DISTINCT VIEWS ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ

  When the user says "add X to [view]", match to one of these three ÔÇö do NOT
  conflate them. All three are active simultaneously during a session.

  1. DevVis  (Device Visibility floating panel ÔÇö inside Topology Sidebar)
       File:     Sidebar-js.html
       Toggle:   toggleDevVisMinimize()
       Purpose:  Per-device show/hide in the topology canvas (hides port cards +
                 D3 nodes). Also has an int_mode row filter with SHORT labels
                 (l2ea, l2etÔÇª) for compact display.
       Scope:    Topology canvas only ÔÇö has no effect on the Google Sheet.

  2. SheetVis  (Sheet View modeless panel ÔÇö inside Google Sheet)
       File:     SheetAssistPanel.html
       Opens:    showSheetAssistPanel()
       Purpose:  (a) Device visibility: hides/shows sheet ROW groups per device.
                 (b) Column selector: shows/hides sheet COLUMNS.
                 (c) Row filters: ip_type (p2p/gw/blank), int_mode, svi ÔÇö all
                     operate on sheet row visibility via refreshSheetRowVisibility().
       Scope:    Google Sheet only ÔÇö has no effect on the topology canvas.

  3. Sheet View menu  (TopoAssist ÔåÆ Sheet View submenu ÔÇö GAS menu bar)
       File:     Code.gs  (onOpen addSubMenu + view functions)
       Calls:    applyCustomView([...keys]) + showSheetAssistPanel()
       Purpose:  Column-visibility PRESETS that show a named subset of columns.
                 Each item is a one-click "view mode" for the sheet.
       Current presets:
         L1: Interface         ÔåÆ ['int']
         L1: Transceiver       ÔåÆ ['int', 'xcvr_type', 'et_speed', 'xcvr_speed']
         L1: Speed             ÔåÆ ['int', 'xcvr_type', 'et_speed', 'xcvr_speed']
         L1.5: Port Channel    ÔåÆ ['int', 'po']
         L2/L3: Mode           ÔåÆ ['int', 'po', 'sp_mode']
         L2/L3: Vlan           ÔåÆ ['int', 'po', 'sp_mode', 'vlan']
         L2/L3: SVI            ÔåÆ ['int', 'po', 'sp_mode', 'vlan', 'svi_vlan']
         L2/L3: IP             ÔåÆ ['int', 'po', 'sp_mode', 'vlan', 'svi_vlan', 'ip_type']
         Custom View...        ÔåÆ opens SheetVis panel (view 2)
       Scope:    Google Sheet column visibility only.

  DISAMBIGUATION RULE:
    "add X filter/row filter"          ÔåÆ SheetVis (2) ÔÇö row visibility
    "add X to the filter panel"        ÔåÆ SheetVis (2) ÔÇö row filter section
    "add X view" / "add X preset"      ÔåÆ Sheet View menu (3) ÔÇö applyCustomView preset
    "add X to the menu"                ÔåÆ Sheet View menu (3)
    "show/hide X in topology"          ÔåÆ DevVis (1)
    References to "L2/L3: SVI, Vlan, Mode" existing items ÔåÆ Sheet View menu (3)

SECTION 1: PROJECT OVERVIEW
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ÔöÇÔöÇ MANAGEMENT SUMMARY ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ

TopoAssist is an Arista lab day-0 automation tool built into Google Sheets.

It lets engineers go from a blank rack to a fully configured, verified network
without touching the CLI manually:

  1. Document  ÔÇö capture physical cabling, transceivers, and port assignments
                 in a structured sheet
  2. Visualize ÔÇö see the live topology diagram and trace VLANs across the network
  3. Validate  ÔÇö flag wrong cables, speed mismatches, and config errors before
                 deployment
  4. Generate  ÔÇö produce device configs (interfaces, BGP, OSPF, VXLAN/EVPN,
                 MLAG) automatically from the sheet data
  5. Push      ÔÇö deploy configs directly to Arista EOS devices with dry-run,
                 commit, and verify phases
  6. Audit     ÔÇö confirm post-deploy that every device matches the intended design

Net result: lab bring-up that used to take days of manual CLI work is reduced to
filling in a spreadsheet and clicking a button. This reduces engineer time on
day-0 activities by a minimum of 2ÔÇô5 days and delivers a working base setup.

ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ

TopoAssist is a Google Apps Script (GAS) day-0 lab workbench embedded in a
Google Spreadsheet. It covers the full lifecycle of bringing up an Arista EOS
lab ÔÇö from physical cabling verification through config generation, push, and
post-deploy auditing.

ÔöÇÔöÇ CORE CAPABILITIES ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ

  Cabling Report
    Export the full physical cabling topology from the sheet as a structured
    table (CSV / Markdown). Includes port, speed, transceiver type, breakout
    grouping, and cable-group compression (e.g. Et14/1-4 as a single QSFP-DD
    row). Snake self-loop cables are excluded automatically.

  Wrong Cabling Report / Cabling Audit
    Flag incorrect or mismatched cables via the Configuration Audit engine:
    - Speed mismatch between et_speed_ (EOS-reported) and xcvr_speed_ (expected)
    - xcvr_type Ôåö et_speed mismatch (transceiver native speed Ôëá actual speed)
    - Missing xcvr_speed_ when breakout is likely (Rule 5 orange highlight)
    - MLAG peer-link missing, asymmetric, or wrong port-channel
    Conditional formatting rules colour the sheet live so mismatches are visible
    without opening any modal.

  Topology Visualization
    Interactive canvas diagram rendered with D3.js inside the sidebar. Devices
    are nodes; cables are edges coloured by layer (underlay, overlay, MLAG,
    snake). Features: drag-to-reposition, zoom/pan, node search/highlight,
    VLAN trace (colour-highlights all ports carrying a VLAN), topology filter
    (by device name, VLAN, internal VLAN), PNG export, dark/light theme toggle.

  Auto Config Generation
    One-click per-device EOS configuration generation from the sheet data:
    - Interface config  ÔÇö switchport (access/trunk), L3, sub-interface, SVI
    - Underlay          ÔÇö BGP (eBGP, unnumbered, RFC-5549) / OSPF / OSPFv3
    - Overlay           ÔÇö VXLAN (L2/L3 VNI), EVPN (IPv4/IPv6)
    - MLAG              ÔÇö peer-link, MLAG domain, keepalive, SVI
    - Snake Test        ÔÇö bidirectional L3 VRF chain with static ARP + routes
                          for traffic-generator connectivity (EP1/EP2 endpoints)
    IP addressing is formula-driven from configurable base octets (P2P /31s,
    GW SVIs, Loopback /32s). BGP ASN base is configurable. 16 network-family
    flags (INT_IPV4, INT_IPV6, INT_IPV6_UNNUM, GW_IPV4, GW_IPV6, BGP├ù4,
    OSPF├ù3, VXLAN├ù2, EVPN├ù2) let you mix/match protocol families per topology.
    Supports IXIA/Spirent traffic generators as non-Arista endpoints.

  Config Push
    Directly push generated configs to live Arista EOS devices via
    device_bridge.py (local Python bridge, SSH or eAPI):
    - 3-phase push: dry-run diff ÔåÆ commit ÔåÆ verify
    - Idempotent: section cleaners wipe stale BGP/OSPF/interface state first
    - Single-device push from topology node, or Generate All ÔåÆ Push All
    - Live phase tracker with elapsed timer; "already in sync" auto-closes
    - Abort-stale-sessions cleans orphan SSH sessions before each push

  Auditing
    Post-deploy configuration audit checks across all devices:
    A. Port-channel link count consistency
    B. MLAG peer-link symmetry (same PO on both peers)
    C. Duplicate P2P VLANs across device pairs
    D. Speed mismatch (et_speed_ Ôëá xcvr_speed_ when both set)
    E. VLAN range validity (1ÔÇô4094)
    F. VLAN conflicts across trunk ports on the same PO
    G. Native VLAN on non-trunk port
    H. MLAG peer-link missing / required
    I. Po mismatch / asymmetric link count
    J. nv<N> native-VLAN token on non-trunk port
    K. Internal VLAN conflict (EOS-reserved VLANs via device bridge data)
    M. Stale SVI: svi_vlan_ filled but mode is l3-* (SVI only valid on L2 modes)
    N. Stale VLANs: vlan_ has 2+ VLANs (comma or range) but mode is pure l3-* non-sub-int
       (single VLAN is allowed on l3-et/l3-po)
    O. Stale VRF: vrf_ filled but mode is l2-* with no SVI
    P. Incomplete Xcvr: xcvr_speed_ filled but xcvr_type_ is blank
    Q. Missing VLAN: mode is l3-et/l3-po but vlan_ is blank (required for IP derivation)

  Topology Search
    Instant filter across all devices, ports, VLANs, descriptions, and internal
    VLANs. Matching nodes are highlighted on the canvas; non-matching nodes are
    dimmed. VLAN trace mode colours all ports carrying a given VLAN (including
    EOS-internal VLANs surfaced via device bridge). Device bridge search also
    matches on internal VLAN numbers.

  Device Bridge (live device connectivity)
    device_bridge.py ÔÇö local Python HTTP bridge (SSH + eAPI dual path):
    - LLDP neighbor pull ÔåÆ auto-populates cabling sheet from live topology
    - Device status check: EOS version, interface list, internal VLANs,
      bridge MAC (for snake test ARP config)
    - Config push (3-phase) and push-all workflows

ÔöÇÔöÇ SCOPE ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ

  LAB TOOL ONLY ÔÇö not for production.
  IPv6 syntax intentionally deviates from strict Arista EOS syntax to align
  with IPv4 for lab testing convenience.
  IXIA/Spirent traffic generators appear as non-Arista device rows in the sheet.

SECTION 2: FILE STRUCTURE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All files live in: ~/claude/projects/topoassist/

  Code.gs             ÔÇö Server-side GAS. All backend logic:
                        Menu, column views, schema, sheet rebuild engine,
                        visual formatting engine, topology calculation,
                        config generation (BGP, MLAG, VXLAN/EVPN), snapshots,
                        device manager, IP preferences, global config editor.

  Sidebar.html        ÔÇö HTML entry point for the modeless dialog (sidebar).
                        Includes CSS/JS via GAS include() helper.
                        Renders multiple UI modes: topology, manager, schema,
                        view_custom, all driven by template.initialMode.

  Sidebar-css.html    ÔÇö All CSS for the sidebar UI. Must use JetBrains Mono
                        explicitly on EVERY element (buttons, inputs, labels,
                        status text). Elements do NOT inherit from body in GAS.

  Sidebar-js.html     ÔÇö All client-side JavaScript. D3.js topology rendering,
                        SortableJS for drag-and-drop, html2canvas for PNG export,
                        edit mode, validation mode, config generation calls,
                        schema manager, device manager, search/filter, polling.

  UserGuide.html      ÔÇö In-app documentation page (modal dialog). Covers:
                        Quick Start (4 steps), full toolbar reference (primary +
                        secondary rows) with actual inline SVGs copied from
                        Sidebar.html ÔÇö each icon wrapped in .icon-cell (28x28
                        bordered div) for visual accuracy. Keyboard shortcuts,
                        visual color coding (connection colors, MLAG borders,
                        conditional dimming, device labels), sheet/schema
                        management, column visibility
                        views, checkpoints, config generation (MLAG, IP
                        addressing, auto-description rules, tech stack, global
                        config template), audit engine, and tips.

  SheetAssistPanel.html ÔÇö Merged "Sheet View" modeless dialog (490├ù420px). Two-column
                        layout: LEFT = device visibility (Devices panel), RIGHT = column
                        view selector (Columns panel). Replaces both the old 240├ù380 sheet
                        assist panel and the separate Custom View dialog. Opened via
                        showSheetAssistPanel() or the "Custom View..." menu item.

  INSTRUCTIONS_topoassist.txt ÔÇö This file. Updated on every code change.

  device_bridge.py    ÔÇö Local Python HTTP bridge. Runs on bus-home. Handles
                        /health, /lldp, /devstatus, /pushconfig endpoints.
                        NOT deployed to GAS ÔÇö run directly: python3 device_bridge.py

  .claude/commands/
    version-bump.md      ÔÇö /version-bump: check VERSION sync between device_bridge.py
                           and the embedded template in Sidebar-js.html (downloadBridgeScript())
    check-deploy.md      ÔÇö /check-deploy: list files modified this session, grouped by
                           deployment target (GAS upload vs local run)
    check-userguide.md   ÔÇö /check-userguide: check if UserGuide.html needs updating
                           based on changes made this session
    check-constraints.md ÔÇö /check-constraints: verify all Section 24 hard design constraints
                           (canonicalizeInterface sync, generateConfig param count,
                           hasKey usage, VERSION sync, no MLAG heuristic)

  CLAUDE.md           ÔÇö Loaded at session start. Contains Winnow usage rules for
                        EOS/Arista questions.

SECTION 3: GOOGLE APPS SCRIPT DEPLOYMENT
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

DEPLOY METHOD (bus-home, 2026-04-19+):
  clasp is configured for direct push from bus-home. No manual copy-paste needed.

  Files:
    ~/claude/projects/topoassist/.clasp.json   ÔÇö script ID + rootDir (committed)
    ~/claude/projects/topoassist/appsscript.json ÔÇö GAS manifest (committed)

  Push all 7 GAS files:
    cd ~/claude/projects/topoassist && clasp push

  The PostToolUse hook auto-runs clasp push after every GAS file edit.

  Script ID: 1NL5x7CnPy2Rceet87qUTWlYxfqWaRC19pk5f1zpQR6k5FWf53BQ2JfDJ
  GAS Editor: https://script.google.com/u/0/home/projects/1NL5x7CnPy2Rceet87qUTWlYxfqWaRC19pk5f1zpQR6k5FWf53BQ2JfDJ/edit

CLASP AUTH (headless server ÔÇö run once per machine):
  clasp login --no-localhost
  ÔåÆ Prints an OAuth URL. Open it in any browser.
  ÔåÆ After authorizing, Google redirects to localhost:8888/?code=... (browser shows "This site can't be reached").
  ÔåÆ Copy the full URL from the browser address bar and paste it back in the terminal.
  ÔåÆ Credentials saved to ~/.clasprc.json. No expiry ÔÇö persists until revoked.

  Re-auth needed if: ~/.clasprc.json deleted, token revoked, or "Error: 401" on clasp push.

  Enable Apps Script API first (required): https://script.google.com/home/usersettings
    ÔåÆ Toggle "Google Apps Script API" ON.

INITIAL SETUP STEPS (new spreadsheet):
  1. Create a new Google Spreadsheet.
  2. Open Extensions > Apps Script.
  3. Create 5 files matching the names above (Code.gs already exists by default).
  4. Paste code from each file into the corresponding Apps Script file.
  5. Save. Reload the spreadsheet.
  6. Run onOpen() once to authorize permissions.
  7. The "TopoAssist" menu will appear in the spreadsheet.

PERMISSIONS REQUIRED:
  - SpreadsheetApp (read/write spreadsheet)
  - PropertiesService (script, document, user properties for state)
  - CacheService (user cache for topology caching)
  - HtmlService (sidebar/dialog rendering)
  - SpreadsheetApp.getUi() (menus, prompts, alerts, toasts)

EXTERNAL LIBRARIES (CDN, loaded in Sidebar.html):
  - D3.js v7.8.5          ÔÇö Topology visualization
  - SortableJS v1.15.0    ÔÇö Drag-and-drop device ordering in manager
  - html2canvas v1.4.1    ÔÇö PNG export of topology
  - JetBrains Mono (Google Fonts) ÔÇö Monospace font for all UI

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 3B: GLOBAL UI RULES (apply to ALL UI elements, always)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These rules apply to every UI element in every file. Treat violations as bugs.

1. MONOSPACE FONT
   Every <button>, <input>, <select>, <textarea>, <label>, and status text must
   explicitly set: font-family: "JetBrains Mono"
   Elements do NOT inherit font-family from body in GAS/browser ÔÇö always set it.

2. UI/UX SYMMETRY
   Spacing, padding, alignment, and sizing must be consistent and balanced:
   - Matching elements in the same context must have identical padding/margin
   - Button/input sizes within a group must be uniform
   - Alignment must be consistent (no accidental mix of left/center/right)
   - Visual weight must be balanced across all sides of a layout
   - Hover/focus/active interaction states must be consistent across similar controls
   When adding one element to a group, check all siblings for symmetry.

4. HD ICONS (SVG only)
   All icons must be inline SVG vectors ÔÇö never Unicode characters (ÔùÄ Ôûñ Ô£ª Ôÿ░ Ô£ò)
   or emoji used as visual icons. Unicode chars blur at small sizes and misalign.
   - Use <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" ...> for toolbar icon-toggle
   - Use <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" ...> for larger icon-btn
   - Always set stroke="currentColor" so icons inherit button color for hover/active
   - Icon set: Feather/Lucide (already used throughout TopoAssist)
   - If a Unicode char was used as icon: replace with SVG + remove font-size CSS

3. CANVAS BOUNDARY
   No modal, tooltip, dropdown, panel, or overlay may render outside the
   viewport/canvas boundary. The GAS sidebar/dialog is ~490px wide.
   - All widths must use min(Xpx, calc(100vw - Npx)) not hard-coded px
   - Fixed/absolute positioned elements must include max-width: calc(100vw - Npx)
   - overflow: hidden on containers that have children which could overflow
   - Inputs that expand on focus must use max-width relative to parent, not fixed px
   - Never use min-width larger than the expected viewport width (490px)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 4: GOOGLE SHEET STRUCTURE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The working sheet name defaults to "PortMapping". Stored in ScriptProperties
under key 'TARGET_SHEET_NAME'. Can be renamed via TopoAssist > Sheet View >
Change Sheet Name.

ROW 1: Device Names (merged across their attribute columns)
ROW 2: Attribute headers in format: <attribute_key>_<DeviceName>
  Example: int_Leaf1, po_Leaf1, sp_mode_Leaf1, ..., int_Leaf2, po_Leaf2, ...
ROWS 3+: Data rows (one row per physical port / connection)

ATTRIBUTE SCHEMA (DEFAULT ORDER):
  NOTE: Keys below are the internal schema keys (no trailing underscore).
  Column headers in the sheet are formatted as <key>_<DeviceName> (e.g. int_Leaf1).
  Key         Label           Dropdown Options
  -------     -----------     ----------------
  int         Interface       (free text: Et1, Po10, Vl10, Lo0, Ma0)
  po          Port-Channel    (free text: Po10, Po100)
  sp_mode     Mode            l2-et-access, l2-et-trunk, l2-po-access, l2-po-trunk,
                              l3-et-int, l3-et-sub-int, l3-po-int, l3-po-sub-int
  vlan        VLANs           (free text: 10, 10,20, 10-20; add nv<N> for trunk native VLAN e.g. 10,20,nv100)
  svi_vlan    SVI VLANs       all (all VLANs in vlan_), <id> or <id,id> (specific VLANs only)
  ip_type     IP Type         p2p, gw
  vrf         VRF             (free text)
  speed       Speed           auto, 1g, 10g, 25g, 40g-4, 50g-1, 50g-2, 100g-1,
                              100g-2, 100g-4, 200g-1, 200g-2, 200g-4, 400g-2,
                              400g-4, 400g-8, 800g-4, 800g-8, 1.6t-8, sfp-1000baset
  encoding    FEC             fire-code, reed-solomon
  xcvr        Transceiver     (free text: QSFP28, SFP+, OSFP, etc.)
  desc        Description     (free text)
  sd          SD              (free text)
  dp-pp-mp_   DP-PP-MP        (free text)

NON-ARISTA DEVICES (IXIA, Spirent, traffic generators):
  - Detected by name containing: ixia, traffic, spirent, tgen (case-insensitive)
  - Or explicitly registered as non-arista via Device Manager
  - Get only ONE column: int_<DeviceName>
  - No attribute columns, no config generation

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 6: UI MODES (Sidebar.html / initialMode)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Sidebar.html template is multipurpose, driven by template.initialMode:

  'topology'      ÔÇö Main network topology visualizer (1600x900 dialog)
  'manager'       ÔÇö Device Manager (600x800 dialog)
  'schema'        ÔÇö Column & Formatting manager (700x800 dialog)
  'view_custom'   ÔÇö Custom column visibility manager (now merged into SheetAssistPanel)

STANDALONE SHEET-SIDE PANELS (separate HTML files, not Sidebar modes):
  SheetAssistPanel.html ÔÇö Merged Sheet View (490├ù420). Two-column layout combining
                          device visibility (left) and column view selector (right).
                          Opened via showSheetAssistPanel() or "Custom View..." menu item.

SHEET MANAGER PANEL (SheetAssistPanel.html):
  Light theme (white body, #f1f5f9 header). Modeless dialog, 490├ù420px, title "Sheet View".
  Two-column layout: col-left (230px, border-right) = Devices, col-right (flex:1) = Columns.
  Shared status bar at bottom. Minimize collapses panel-body and status-bar, sets height to 36px.

  GLOBAL SEARCH ÔÇö single search bar between header and body (id=searchRow, input id=globalSearch).
    filterAll() filters both .device-item (by data-name/data-hostname) and .col-item (by data-label).
    Called on oninput; also called after renderDevices() and renderColItems(). Hidden on minimize.

  LEFT COLUMN ÔÇö Devices:
    SHOW ALL / HIDE ALL bulk buttons. Scrollable device list.
    Each device row: eye icon ÔåÆ toggle(), device name ÔåÆ navigate().
    Eye and name use event.stopPropagation(); only their own handler fires.

  RIGHT COLUMN ÔÇö Columns:
    SHOW ALL / HIDE ALL bulk buttons ÔÇö same style as device panel (green/orange, btn-bulk classes).
    2-column grid (grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr) of column type items with eye icons ÔÇö same
    visual as device items (eye-open green = visible, eye-closed gray = hidden, line-through label).
    Every toggle auto-applies via applyCustomView(visibleKeys) instantly. No Apply button, no presets.
    Mandatory first item (always visible, dimmed, not clickable).
    Loads via getSchemaConfig() ÔåÆ getViewPreferences() on panel open; state kept in visibleKeys[].

GAS FUNCTIONS for Sheet View (Code.gs):
  showSheetAssistPanel()     ÔÇö Opens SheetAssistPanel.html (490├ù420 modeless dialog, "Sheet View");
                               calls ensureOnChangeTrigger() + ensureOnOpenTrigger() in try/catch
  getSheetDeviceList()       ÔÇö Returns [{name, hostname, isVisible, isArista}] ÔÇö isVisible from SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN; isArista = d.type !== 'non-arista'
  toggleSheetDevice(name)    ÔÇö Updates SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN, calls applyCustomView(getViewPreferences()) + refreshSheetRowVisibility()
  showAllSheetDevices()      ÔÇö Clears SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN; shows all device columns; refreshes rows
  hideAllSheetDevices()      ÔÇö Writes all device names to SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN; hides all device columns; refreshes rows

TOPOLOGY TOOLBAR (primary row):
  - Minimize/restore button
  - Refresh button (fetchData)
  - W/G/O/T number inputs (card width, device gap, cable offset, cable top margin)
  - Sort controls: SHEET | MODE | IP | ALPHA
  - Edit mode toggle (pencil icon)
  - Group rect mode toggle (rectangle icon)
  - Bold text toggle
  - Technology stack modal (BGP/VXLAN/EVPN toggles)
  - IP Config modal
  - PNG download (html2canvas)
  - Cabling export modal (openCablingModal):
      Ô¼í Topology Patching List ÔÇö Download Topology Patching (downloadCablingReport('netlist'))
                               ÔÇö Copy CSV (copyCablingCsv()) / Copy Markdown (copyCablingMarkdown())
                                 both topology-order; sub-buttons sit below Download, 8px margin-top
      Ôù╗ Device Patching List  ÔÇö Download Device Patching (downloadCablingReport('device'))
  - Help/shortcuts modal
  - Dark/light theme toggle
  - Audit/validation mode toggle (shield icon)
  - Toolbar collapse toggle

TOPOLOGY TOOLBAR (secondary row):
  - View mode: ÔùÄ Simple (holistic) | Ôûñ Linear | Ô£ª Flexible (physics/D3 force)
  - Search/filter input (supports VLAN tracing with "v<number>" syntax)
  - Strict search checkbox
  - Status text (device count, link count)

TOPOLOGY TOOLBAR (copy strip):
  - Shows after clicking a link/device
  - Split buttons: Device | Left | Right
  - Each has Copy (copies EOS config to clipboard) and View (opens config modal)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 7: TOPOLOGY VIEW MODES
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LINEAR VIEW (default):
  - Device cards in fixed sheet order (left to right)
  - Each device shows a list of port rows
  - Color-coded cables drawn as SVG lines connecting matching ports
  - Suitable for cabling/patching documentation

DEVICE CARD COLUMN LAYOUT (port rows inside each node card):
  Grid: 62px 1fr 30px 40px 25px
  Columns: Et | Mode | Cat | Po | St
    Et   (62px) ÔÇö interface name; left-aligned header + data (62px holds up to ~9-char names like "et6/66/66")
    Mode (1fr)  ÔÇö sp_mode_ value (routed/trunk/accessÔÇª); left-aligned; truncates with ellipsis
    Cat  (30px) ÔÇö port category pill: P2P (violet) / GW (amber) / L2 (gray); centered
    Po   (40px) ÔÇö port-channel ("Po1", "Po10", blank if none); left-aligned header + data
    St   (25px) ÔÇö status dot (connected=green, disconnected=gray); centered
  Cat values: "P2P", "GW", "L2" (previously L2 showed "-"; now consistently labeled).
  Header alignment: .node-cols-header has border-left:3px solid transparent (matches
    port-row's border-left:3px) so Et/Mode/Po headers align with data rows.
    nth-child(1,2,4) overridden to justify-content:flex-start to match data alignment.
  Sort button "CAT" (id=btnSortIp, changeSort('priority')): sorts P2PÔåÆGWÔåÆL2 (was "IP").

SIMPLE (HOLISTIC) VIEW:
  - One node per device, rendered as a box
  - Lines between connected device pairs (one line per unique pair)
  - Group rects can be drawn over it to label logical groups
  - Suitable for high-level topology understanding

FLEXIBLE VIEW:
  - D3 force-directed graph
  - Nodes are draggable, positions are saved per session
  - Same visual style as Simple view but physics-based

DEVICE NODE LABELS:
  SPINE, LEAF, HARNESS, TRANSIT, DUT, IXIA, SPIRENT
  Each has a distinct background/text/border color scheme.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 8: TOPOLOGY ENGINE (calculateGlobalTopology)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Server-side function in Code.gs. Reads the full sheet data and headers.
Returns:
  mlagConfigPorts ÔÇö Set<"DeviceName:PoX">  Port-Channels detected as MLAG config ports
  peerLinkPorts   ÔÇö Set<"DeviceName:PoX" or "DeviceName:EtX">  MLAG peer-link ports
  mlagPeerMap     ÔÇö Map<deviceName, partnerName>  MLAG pair lookup (both directions)
  globalLinkMap   ÔÇö Map<"DeviceName:Port", {dev, port}>  full topology link index
  debugLogs       ÔÇö Array<string>  diagnostic messages (not returned to client)

MLAG DETECTION (STRICT COUNT = 4):
  - A Port-Channel number is considered MLAG if it appears across >= 4 rows
    in the entire sheet (counting both int_ and po_ columns)
  - This is intentional: no non-EOS device will be the MLAG client
  - Do NOT change this threshold

PEER-LINK DETECTION:
  - A physical link between two MLAG peers is tagged as a peer-link
  - Identified from the topology engine, not from sheet data alone

KEY HELPER: hasKey(setObj, key)
  - Case-insensitive Set/Map lookup
  - Always use hasKey() instead of .has() when device names are involved
  - Device names from the sheet are original-cased; keys in Sets use lowercase

DATA_VERSION polling:
  - getDataVersion() returns a timestamp from ScriptProperties
  - Client polls this every few seconds to detect sheet changes
  - On change: fetchData(false) is called to refresh topology without forcing

TOPOLOGY CACHE:
  - getTopologyData() caches the full topology JSON in CacheService.getUserCache()
  - Cache key: 'TOPO_' + DATA_VERSION
  - Invalidated on forceSync or when DATA_VERSION changes

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 9: SHEET REBUILD ENGINE (rebuildSheet)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Core function: rebuildSheet(forcedOrderList, forcedSchemaList, applyFormatting)

STAGES:
  1. BACKUP ÔÇö reads all existing data into memory (values + formulas)
  2. ANALYZE ÔÇö maps existing data to device/attribute keys
  3. GENERATE ÔÇö builds new Row 1 (device names), Row 2 (headers), body data
  4. COMMIT ÔÇö writes to sheet (always runs)
  5. VALIDATION ÔÇö applies dropdown validations (always runs)
  6. STRUCTURAL FORMATTING ÔÇö font, alignment, borders, merges, adaptive column widths
                              (width = max(80, ceil(header.length * 7) + 16); Consolas 10px
                               Ôëê 7px/char + 16px padding; auto-adapts to device name length)
  7. COLOR APPLICATION ÔÇö device header colors (golden angle hslToHex),
                          connection backgrounds, conditional format rules

SYNC_STATUS PROGRESS (written to CacheService.getUserCache() at each stage):
  Phase 1/4: Reading sheet data  ÔåÆ  Phase 2/4: Writing to sheet
  Phase 3/4: Applying formatting ÔåÆ  Phase 4/4: Restoring column view  ÔåÆ  Sync complete
  Polled every 600ms via getSyncStatus() by three callers:
    - triggerSyncOnly() (Force Sync button)
    - saveSchemaChanges() ÔÇö structural change path only (isStructuralChange=true)
    - saveDeviceChanges() ÔÇö slow path only (isStructureDirty=true, calls processDeviceBatch)
  All three show global loading overlay during poll and hide it on completion/error.
  SCOPING NOTE (saveSchemaChanges): syncPollTimer is declared as `let` at function scope
  (null-initialized), NOT inside the withSuccessHandler callback, so the 30s schemaLockTimer
  timeout handler can clearInterval(syncPollTimer)+hideGlobalLoading() if server hangs.

POST-REBUILD VISIBILITY RESTORE (end of stage 7):
  rebuildSheet() calls refreshSheetRowVisibility() THEN applyCustomView(getViewPreferences()).
  ORDER IS CRITICAL: refreshSheetRowVisibility() calls ensureDummyColumn() first, inserting
  _sys_ at col 1 and shifting device columns to col 2+. applyCustomView() then reads the
  correct layout (col A = _sys_ always visible, cols B+ = device columns to show/hide).
  If applyCustomView() runs first (before _sys_ exists), col A is a device column that
  gets locked visible, and _sys_ is never created ÔÇö the bug that caused force sync to
  delete col A without restore.
  Reason: clearContent() in stage 4 wipes _sys_ and all column hide state; without both
  calls in the correct order, _sys_ stays gone and row visibility is broken after every sync.
  NOTE: stage 4 clear chain must include .clearNote() ÔÇö clearContent()+clearFormat() do NOT
  clear notes. Without it, the _sys_ note persists on col A after clear, then when
  ensureDummyColumn() inserts the new _sys_ column (pushing device data to col B), both
  col A (new _sys_) and col B (old col A with ghost note) show "Managed by TopoAssist".
  Wrapped in try/catch so a visibility error does not block the success toast.

SAFETY:
  - If new body data is empty but backup had rows ÔåÆ abort with error + rollback
  - On any error: rolls back to backup data
  - Orphaned columns (not in schema but in sheet) are detected client-side before sync;
    user sees confirm() with per-column data-loss warning; decision passed as deleteOrphans flag

DEVICE HEADER COLORS:
  - Uses golden angle (137.5┬░) hue rotation: hue = (200 + i * 137.5) % 360
  - Pastel: HSL with saturation=85, lightness=88

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 10: VISUAL FORMATTING ENGINE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

applyVisualFormatting():
  1. Reads data and headers from sheet
  2. Calls calculateGlobalTopology() for MLAG/peer-link detection
  3. Calls calculateConnectionBackgrounds() ÔåÆ returns color matrix + MLAG ranges
  4. Applies background color matrix to data range
  5. Applies black SOLID_MEDIUM borders to MLAG cells
  6. Calls buildConditionalRules() ÔåÆ applies all conditional format rules
  7. Sets Consolas font, size 10, middle/center alignment

CONNECTION COLORS (calculateConnectionBackgrounds):
  - Pairs up columns in order: every 2 filled int_ cells = one cable pair
  - Physical links: pastel color derived from port name hash
  - Port-Channel (regular): distinct pastel color from Po number
  - MLAG Port-Channel: different pastel + black border
  - Peer-Link: separate color
  - Orphan (unpaired): white (#ffffff)

CONDITIONAL FORMAT RULES (buildConditionalRules) ÔÇö 6 priority tiers (first = highest):
  Priority 1 ÔÇö AUDIT RED (#fca5a5/#991b1b): stale/conflicting field with int_ filled
    A1: po_ filled + ET mode
    A2: svi_vlan_ filled + l3-* mode
    A3: ip_type_ filled + l2-* mode + no SVI
    A4: vlan_ has 2+ VLANs (contains comma or dash) + pure l3-* non-sub-int
        (single VLAN on l3-et/l3-po is NOT flagged ÔÇö needed for IP derivation)
    A5: vrf_ filled + l2-* mode + no SVI
    A6: xcvr_speed_ filled + xcvr_type_ missing ÔåÆ RED on xcvr_speed_ (paired with audit P)
  Priority 2 ÔÇö MISSING AMBER (#fef3c7/#92400e):
    A7: sp_mode_ empty when int_ is filled (mode required)
    A8: vlan_ empty + mode is l3-et or l3-po (required for IP derivation; paired with audit Q)
  Priority 3 ÔÇö INACTIVE GRAY (#f1f5f9/#cbd5e1):
    N1: int_ empty ÔåÆ all SCHEMA_KEYS columns for that device (single multi-range rule)
  Priority 4 ÔÇö N/A GRAY (#e2e8f0/#cbd5e1): field not applicable for current mode
    N/A-1: svi_vlan_ gray when mode is l3-* (A2 overrides RED when filled)
    N/A-2: po_ gray when mode is l2-et-* or l3-et-* (A1 overrides RED when filled)
    N/A-3: ip_type_ gray when mode is l2-* + no SVI (A3 overrides RED when filled)
    N/A-4: REMOVED ÔÇö vlan_ is needed for ALL l3 modes (IP derivation on l3-et/l3-po,
           dot1q tag on sub-int). A4 still catches 2+ VLANs on pure l3.
    N/A-5: xcvr columns gray when mode is Po ÔÇö Po has no physical transceiver; xcvr_ is
           Et-only. Truly N/A: no RED override, no audit needed.
    N/A-6: vrf_ gray when mode is l2-* + no SVI (A5 overrides RED when filled)
  Priority 5 ÔÇö QUALITY WARNINGS: W1 (amber), W2 (pale-orange)
  Priority 6 ÔÇö MEMBER PORT: italic + muted text

IMPORTANT: After editing buildConditionalRules, user must click Force Sync
(toolbar button in the sidebar) for conditional format changes to take effect.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 11: CONFIG GENERATION
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Entry point: generateConfig(portName, d, ipPrefs, seenPos, netSettings)
  portName    ÔÇö interface name (e.g. "Et1", "Po10", "Et1.100")
  d           ÔÇö data object with all attribute values for that row
  ipPrefs     ÔÇö IP preferences (base subnets, VRFs, etc.)
  seenPos     ÔÇö Set of already-generated Port-Channels (prevents duplicates)
  netSettings ÔÇö IP family flags object from getNetworkSettings(); passed to
                generateComplexL3Block() to gate IPv6/OSPF/unnumbered commands.
                INVARIANT: MUST be passed by every caller. Omitting silently drops
                per-protocol commands (IPv6 addressing, OSPF per-interface, etc.).

DESCRIPTION LOGIC (9-rule system):
  Rule 1: Manual override (d.desc_ is set) ÔåÆ use as-is
  Rule 2: Regular physical ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev-PeerPort"
  Rule 3: Physical peer-link (standalone) ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev-PeerPort-MLAG-PEER-LINK"
  Rule 4: Physical child of regular Po ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev-PeerPort-PoX"
  Rule 5: Po (regular) ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev [& PeerDev2]"
  Rule 6: Physical child of MLAG Po ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev-PeerPort-PoX"
  Rule 7: MLAG Po ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev & PeerDev2 (MLAG)"
  Rule 8: Physical peer-link child of Po ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev-PeerPort-PoX"
  Rule 9: Po peer-link ÔåÆ "-> PeerDev (MLAG-PEER-LINK)"

INVALID CONFIG GUARD:
  MLAG + any L3 mode (l3-*) is INVALID on Arista EOS.
  generateConfig() returns an ERROR comment block instead of real config.
  generateComplexL3Block() also guards: returns "" for all l3-* modes with MLAG.

OSPF UNDERLAY (generateOSPF + generateOSPFv3):
  generateOSPF(deviceSheetIndex, bgpNeighbors) ÔÇö OSPFv2 (router ospf 1):
  - Generates OSPF process blocks for all VRFs (area 0, single-area leaf-spine).
  - router-id: <id>.<id>.<id>.<id> (same loopback pattern as BGP); shared across
    all VRF OSPF instances (EOS leaf-spine convention).
  - VRF grouping: non-MLAG P2P interfaces are grouped by p.vrf from peerParams.
    DEFAULT VRF ÔåÆ router ospf 1
    Non-default VRF ÔåÆ router ospf 1 vrf <name>  (one block per VRF, sorted)
    All blocks use: passive-interface default + no passive-interface per interface,
    bfd default, max-lsa 12000. All emitted in a single 090_OSPF_UNDERLAY string.
  - Vlan4093 always added to the DEFAULT VRF set when an MLAG peer exists.
  - Guard: called only when netSettings.ospf_ipv4 is true.

  generateOSPFv3(deviceSheetIndex, bgpNeighbors) ÔÇö OSPFv3 (router ospf3 1):
  - Mirrors generateOSPF() exactly but uses "router ospf3 1" keyword.
  - Emitted as 091_OSPF3_UNDERLAY block (between OSPFv2 and BGP blocks).
  - Guard: called only when netSettings.ospf_ipv6 is true.

  Per-interface OSPF commands (generateComplexL3Block):
  - OSPFv2 (addOspfV4 = netSettings.ospf_ipv4): ip ospf network point-to-point,
    ip ospf area 0.0.0.0, ip ospf neighbor bfd ÔÇö on all P2P modes:
      l2-* with svi_vlan_: commands on each Vlan<x> SVI
      -sub-int modes:       commands on each <port>.<vlan> sub-interface
      l3-et-int / l3-po-int: commands on the routed interface
  - OSPFv3 (addOspfV6 = netSettings.ospf_ipv6): ipv6 ospf 1 area 0.0.0.0
    added on same P2P interfaces.
  - No VRF guard ÔÇö VRF interfaces are covered by per-VRF process blocks.
  - MLAG guard: generateOSPF/generateOSPFv3 called only when hasP2pForOspf ÔÇö
    at least one non-MLAG peerParam. MLAG-only devices skip (avoids dead process).

BGP EVPN OVERLAY ONLY (generateBGPEvpnOverlay(deviceSheetIndex, deviceName, bgpNeighbors, gwVlans, peerRoles, settings, ipPrefs)):
  - Used when OSPF is underlay + EVPN is enabled
  - Generates overlay-only BGP: loopback-to-loopback peers, no P2P sessions
  - Peer groups: OVERLAY_<PEER>_V4_LO_IP with update-source Loopback0 + ebgp-multihop 3
  - address-family evpn only (no ipv4/ipv6 address families)
  - MLAG partners are filtered out (isMlagOnly check): per EOS design, MLAG peers do
    NOT have BGP EVPN sessions with each other ÔÇö EVPN sessions are spine-only; the
    MLAG peer's Vlan4093 session (underlay only) is handled separately.
    bgpNeighbors always contains the MLAG partner (added by generateMlagConfig), so
    the filter is required to prevent a spurious loopback EVPN session between peers.
  - peerRoles filtering: isPeerEvpn() helper ÔÇö only LEAF/SPINE peers get overlay sessions;
    all other roles (HARNESS, unset, etc.) are skipped; call site passes peerRoles from getDeviceConfig().

AP VLAN GW (int_ = vx1):
  AP VLANs (wireless SSID VLANs from APs tunneling VXLAN to the GW) are VXLAN-domain
  only ÔÇö no physical port carries them. User places "vx1" in the int_ column.
  Multiple vx1 rows allowed ÔÇö one per VRF/VLAN group.
  Only vlan_ and svi_ fields are evaluated for config; vrf_ used for SVI vrf line.
  ip_type_ is NOT used for vx1 rows.

  MLAG + AP VLAN GW: fully supported. MLAG AP VLAN GW pairs share the same anycast VTEP
  (Loopback1) and must have identical vx1 rows (same VLANs/VRFs on both peers).
  EVPN distributes SSID VLANs leaf-to-leaf via Type-2/Type-3 routes; spines are
  underlay-only and never appear in the VXLAN data plane.

  collectDeviceData() special handling for Vx1 (local AND MLAG peer):
    - VLANs from ALL vx1 rows added to allVlans (VLAN DB) AND gwVlans (VNI mapping).
    - gwVlans add is unconditional ÔÇö no ip_type=gw check (ip_type_ unused for vx1 rows).
    - vrf_ collected into vrfs set via existing analyzeRow() (system block creates VRF).
    - MLAG peer Vx1 rows: also handled explicitly (same unconditional add) because
      ip_type_ being empty on peer vx1 rows would cause analyzeRow() to skip gwVlans.

  getDeviceConfig() interface loop ÔÇö Vx1 pre-collection (before main rows.forEach):
    - ALL vx1 rows collected into vx1Entries[] before main loop runs.
    - "Vx1" pre-added to deviceSeenPos ÔåÆ main loop skips all Vx1 rows cleanly.
    - Each entry: if svi_=yes, generates one interface VlanX block per VLAN.
    - vrf_ included as " vrf <name>" line if set (after "interface VlanX", before description).
    - All SVI blocks concatenated into configMap["050_Vx1"] ("AP VLAN SVI").
    - If svi_=no or vlan_ empty: VLANs still feed gwVlans; no SVI block generated.

  SVI format (vlan 510, vrf TENANT_A, gw_v4_first=100, gw_v4_last=1, anycast mode, gw_ipv6=true):
    interface Vlan510
     vrf TENANT_A
     description ANYCAST_GW_TENANT_A_510     ÔåÉ ANYCAST_GW_<vrf>_<vlan> when VRF set
     ip address virtual 100.5.10.1/24        ÔåÉ anycast (gw_l3_type='anycast')
     default ipv6 address virtual            ÔåÉ only when gw_ipv6=true
     ipv6 address virtual 100:5:10::1/64    ÔåÉ only when gw_ipv6=true
     no shutdown

  SVI format (vlan 510, no VRF, VARP mode):
    interface Vlan510
     description ANYCAST_GW_510              ÔåÉ ANYCAST_GW_<vlan> when no VRF
     ip virtual-router address 100.5.10.1    ÔåÉ VARP (gw_l3_type='varp')
     no shutdown

  GW type is controlled by gw_l3_type in network settings:
    anycast (default): ip address virtual  ÔÇö requires EVPN enabled
    varp:              ip virtual-router address ÔÇö requires ip virtual-router mac-address global
  vx1VlanSet: built from all vx1 SVI VLAN claims; passed to generateComplexL3Block() so
    front-panel SVIs for the same VLAN are skipped (vx1 takes precedence).

  VNI mapping (handled by 055_VXLAN block via gwVlans, VNI base from IP+VNI Config):
    vxlan vlan 510 vni <vni_base + 510>  (default base=10000 ÔåÆ vni 10510)

VTEP LEAF DETECTION & STATIC FLOOD LIST:
  computeVtepNames(allDevices, rows, headers, topo) ÔåÆ Set<string>:
    Scans all Arista devices; a device is a VTEP iff role === 'LEAF' || role === 'SPINE'.
    All other roles (HARNESS, unset, etc.) are never VTEPs.
    Called once in getDeviceConfig() when isVxlan=true; result passed to generateVxlanBlock().

  generateVxlanBlock(..., vniBase, vtepNames):
    Signature now includes vtepNames (Set<string>) as last param.
    Static flood list (non-EVPN only): filters allDevices to vtepNames members only.
    Guard: if vtepNames is empty/null, falls back to all Arista devices (safe default).
    MLAG peer always excluded from flood list (shared anycast IP deduped via Set).

MLAG INFRASTRUCTURE BLOCK (generateMlagConfig(localId, partnerObj, peerLinkName, bgpNeighbors, isVxlan, settings)):
  VLANs:
    - vlan 4094: trunk group MLAG_PEER (control plane, restricted to peer-link)
    - vlan 4093: trunk group MLAG_PEER (L3 peering, ALSO restricted to peer-link)
  SVIs:
    - Vlan4094: no autostate + ip address 169.254.0.x/31
    - Vlan4093: no autostate + ip address 169.254.1.x/31 + (ipv6 address when hasMlagIpv6)
      hasMlagIpv6 = !settings || settings.int_ipv6 || settings.int_ipv6_unnum
      (both SVIs need no autostate so they stay up during failover/reload)
    - Vlan4093 when settings.ospf_ipv4=true: adds ip ospf network point-to-point +
      ip ospf area 0.0.0.0 so OSPF adjacency forms directly between MLAG peers
      (Winnow/EOS confirmed required)
  reload-delay order: mlag 300 first, non-mlag 330 second (non-mlag must be higher
    so MLAG ports are established before non-MLAG ports come up)
  Virtual-router MAC: 0011.2233.<hexId> dotted-hex format, derived from lower peer ID.

IP ADDRESSING (VLAN-DERIVED):
  Middle octets derived from VLAN ID.
  Example: VLAN 1050 ÔåÆ .10.50
  Last octet derived from device DID (sequential Arista device index).
  IPv6: intentionally uses same pattern as IPv4 (not strict EOS syntax) ÔÇö LAB ONLY.

  MLAG GW physical IP formula (generateComplexL3Block, ip_type_=gw, isMlag=true):
    phySuffix = gwLastV4 + sheetIndex  (same for V6)
    virtual-router last octet = gwLastV4 (same on both peers)
    Guarantees: (a) physical Ôëá virtual-router since sheetIndex ÔëÑ 1
                (b) physical IPs unique between peers since sheetIndex is unique
    Example: gwLastV4=1, Leaf1(id=1)ÔåÆ.2, Leaf2(id=2)ÔåÆ.3, virtual-routerÔåÆ.1
    Previous bug: phySuffix=sheetIndex bumped by +1 only when ==gwLastV4 ÔÇö caused
    both peers to get the same physical last octet (e.g. Leaf1ÔåÆ.2, Leaf2ÔåÆ.2).

INTERFACE NAMING (Arista EOS):
  Et  ÔåÆ Ethernet
  Po  ÔåÆ Port-Channel
  Vl  ÔåÆ Vlan (SVI)
  Lo  ÔåÆ Loopback
  Ma  ÔåÆ Management

canonicalizeInterface():
  Normalizes interface abbreviations (e.g. "eth1" ÔåÆ "Et1", "po1" ÔåÆ "Po1").
  DUPLICATED INTENTIONALLY in both Code.gs (server) and Sidebar-js.html (client).

IP + VNI CONFIG MODAL (#ipConfigModal):
  Title: "IP + VNI Configuration". Button tooltip: "IP & VNI Config".
  Size: modal-medium (450px). Body: padding 16px, gap 12px.
  Sections: Point-to-Point, Gateway (SVI/Overlay), VXLAN VNI Mapping.
  IPv4 + IPv6 rows within each section wrapped in .ip-section-rows (gap:4px) so
  they cluster tightly together; section-to-section gap remains 12px.
  Info-box has legend grid (formula) + .ip-example line below it:
    "ex VLAN 1500 ÔåÆ octs 15.0 ┬À P2P: 200.15.0.id ┬À GW: 100.15.0.1 ┬À VNI: 10000+1500=11500"
    (demonstrates oct2=floor(vlan/100), oct3=vlan%100 derivation)
  Field ip_vni_base (VNI Base Offset, default 10000).
  openIpConfigModal() populates ip_vni_base from prefs.vni_base.
  saveIpConfig() includes vni_base in the prefs object sent to saveIpPreferences().
  resetIpConfig() resets ip_vni_base to "10000".

IP PREFERENCES STORAGE:
  - Stored in UserProperties (per user, per spreadsheet)
  - getIpPreferences() / saveIpPreferences()
  - Keys: p2p_v4_first, p2p_v4_mask, p2p_v6_first, p2p_v6_mask,
          gw_v4_first, gw_v4_last, gw_v4_mask, gw_v6_first, gw_v6_last, gw_v6_mask,
          vni_base (default '10000')

NETWORK FEATURE FLAGS (IP FAMILY PER PROTOCOL):
  - Stored in DocumentProperties (shared, per-spreadsheet)
  - getNetworkSettings() / saveNetworkSettings()
  - 16 boolean flags (stored as 'true'/'false' strings):
      P2P INTERFACE: INT_IPV4 (default true), INT_IPV6, INT_IPV6_UNNUM
      GATEWAY:       GW_IPV4 (default true), GW_IPV6
      BGP:           BGP_IPV4, BGP_IPV6, BGP_IPV6_UNNUM, BGP_RFC5549
      OSPF:          OSPF_IPV4, OSPF_IPV6, OSPF_IPV6_UNNUM
      VXLAN:         VXLAN_IPV4, VXLAN_IPV6
      EVPN:          EVPN_IPV4, EVPN_IPV6
  - Legacy migration: reads old NET_UNDERLAY/NET_VXLAN/NET_EVPN; INT_IPV4/GW_IPV4
    default true (all legacy projects had IPv4 always); GW_IPV6 defaults to int_ipv6.
  - P2P vs GW are FULLY DECOUPLED in generateComplexL3Block():
      P2P: p2pHasIpv4 (int_ipv4), p2pUseIpv6Unnum (int_ipv6_unnum),
           p2pUseIpv6Explicit (!unnum && int_ipv6)
      GW:  gwHasIpv4 (gw_ipv4), gwHasIpv6 (gw_ipv6)
      GW is ip_type_=gw ÔÇö applies to SVI (l2-* with svi_vlan_), sub-interfaces
      (-sub-int), and L3 routed ports (l3-et-int / l3-po-int). GW NEVER uses
      IPv6 unnumbered ÔÇö explicit IPs required for VARP.
  - IPv6 routing gates:
      hasP2pIpv6 = int_ipv6 || int_ipv6_unnum ÔÇö gates Lo0 IPv6 addr, ipv6 router-id
      hasAnyIpv6 = hasP2pIpv6 || gw_ipv6     ÔÇö gates VRF ipv6 unicast-routing
      generateGlobalBlock: ipv6 unicast-routing gated on int_ipv6||int_ipv6_unnum||gw_ipv6
  - BGP_RFC5549: gates pgV6Int peer groups; valid for any IPv6 P2P mode (link-local
    always present on any IPv6-enabled interface, including unnumbered).
  - addVtepIpv6 in generateVxlanBlock: gated on vxlan_ipv6 ONLY (not ||int_ipv6).
  - Feature derivation in config engine:
      isBgp  = bgp_ipv4 || bgp_ipv6 || bgp_ipv6_unnum || bgp_rfc5549
      isOspf = ospf_ipv4 || ospf_ipv6 || ospf_ipv6_unnum
      isVxlan = (vxlan_ipv4 || vxlan_ipv6) && isVxlanDevice
      isEvpn  = (evpn_ipv4  || evpn_ipv6)  && isEvpnDevice
  - Cross-validation (validateTechSettings() in Sidebar-js.html ÔÇö 4 rules):
      1. gw_ipv6 + no IPv6 routing protocol (bgp_ipv6/rfc5549/bgp_unnum/ospf_ipv6/
         ospf_ipv6_unnum/evpn_ipv4/evpn_ipv6) ÔåÆ error
      2. vxlan_ipv4 + no IPv4 underlay (bgp_ipv4/bgp_unnum/rfc5549/ospf_ipv4) ÔåÆ error
      3. vxlan_ipv6 + no IPv6 underlay (bgp_ipv6/bgp_unnum/rfc5549/ospf_ipv6/
         ospf_ipv6_unnum) ÔåÆ error
      4. evpn (any) + no BGP (any variant) ÔåÆ error
    Errors shown in #techValidationErrors banner; Save button disabled.
    BGP Unnum and RFC5549 count for IPv4 underlay (both negotiate ipv4 unicast AF).
  - UI: Tech modal (#techModal) ÔÇö width 580px:
      GATEWAY (top): chkGwIpv4, chkGwIpv6 ÔÇö always enabled, no protocol gating
      P2P INTERFACE: radio group (name=p2pMode) ÔÇö 5 values:
        ipv4 / ipv6 / ipv6unnum / ipv4ipv6 / ipv4ipv6unnum
      Protocol grid (4 cols, gated by P2P mode):
        BGP: chkBgpIpv4, chkBgpIpv6, chkBgpIpv6Unnum, chkBgpRfc5549
        OSPF: chkOspfIpv4, chkOspfIpv6, chkOspfIpv6Unnum
        VXLAN: chkVxlanIpv4, chkVxlanIpv6
        EVPN: chkEvpnIpv4, chkEvpnIpv6
      TECH_COMPAT (5 entries) + P2P_MODE_FLAGS (5 entries, radioÔåÆ{int_ipv4,int_ipv6,
        int_ipv6_unnum}) defined as module-level constants in Sidebar-js.html.
  - Config blocks: 090_OSPF_UNDERLAY (ospf_ipv4), 091_OSPF3_UNDERLAY (ospf_ipv6)
    both between VXLAN and BGP sections. generateConfig() 5th param (netSettings)
    passed from BOTH getDeviceConfig() AND getTopologyData() (as globalNetSettings).

GLOBAL CONFIG TEMPLATE:
  - Stored in DocumentProperties under key 'GLOBAL_DEVICE_CONFIG_TEMPLATE'
  - Edited via sidebar toolbar button (lines/magnifier SVG, between IP Config and VLAN Summary)
  - Applied as a base template before per-device config generation (via generateGlobalBlock())
  - Sidebar modal #globalCfgModal (modal-std modal-medium): openGlobalCfgModal() loads
    current config via getGlobalConfig(), shows textarea. saveGlobalCfgFromSidebar() saves
    via saveGlobalConfig(), then clears configCache (sole config store) +
    refreshes active device config immediately (same pattern as saveTechSettings).
    closeGlobalCfgModal() hides modal + overlay. No Close button in header ÔÇö footer Cancel
    is the only dismiss control (avoids duplicated close affordances).
  - Find bar (.gcfg-find-bar) sits between modal-header and textarea: search input
    (#globalCfgSearch), match counter (#globalCfgSearchCount), Prev/Next chevron SVG buttons.
    globalCfgSearchUpdate() builds _gcfgMatches[] via indexOf loop. _gcfgJumpTo(idx) uses
    setSelectionRange + scrollTop calculation (linesBefore ├ù lineHeight). Enter=next,
    Shift+Enter=prev, Escape=clear. openGlobalCfgModal() resets all find state on open.
  - Editor area always light mode: wrapper bg #f8fafc, textarea bg #ffffff, color #1e293b,
    border #cbd5e1 (focus: #3b82f6). Hardcoded ÔÇö not CSS vars ÔÇö so readable in both themes.
  - globalCfgModal registered in modalOrder, closeFuncs (topologyKeyHandler), and
    closeAllModals() array so Escape and closeAllModals() dismiss it correctly.

SECTION 12: DEVICE MANAGER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

showDeviceManagerUi() ÔåÆ 600x800 modeless dialog in 'manager' mode.

HEADER: flex row ÔÇö "Device Manager" label (left) + Ô£ò close button (.reorder-header-close)
  on right. Close triggers attemptCloseManager() (warns on unsaved changes).

ADD DEVICES:
  - Text input supports individual names ("Leaf1") or ranges ("Leaf[1-4]")
  - parseAndExpandDevices() handles range expansion with zero-padding support
  - Max 50 devices total, max range size of 50
  - Device types: 'full' (Arista) or 'non-arista'

DEVICE ORDER:
  - Devices can be reordered via SortableJS drag-and-drop
  - Order saved to Document Properties and used for sheet column order
  - On reorder, orphaned schema columns are always preserved (no prompt)
  - Drag resets pendingDeleteIndex to -1 (cancels any in-flight delete confirmation)

DEVICE VISIBILITY (3 independent mechanisms ÔÇö see Section 25 for full detail):
  - Sheet View (temporary): SHEET_VIEW_HIDDEN UserProperties ÔÇö hides sheet columns only
  - Topology View (temporary): in-memory JS Set ÔÇö hides topology nodes only
  - Device Manager (permanent): TOPOLOGY_HIDDEN_DEVICES ScriptProperties ÔÇö persistent node visibility

DEVICE DID (Device ID):
  - Sequential integer assigned to each Arista device
  - Used for last-octet IP derivation
  - Non-Arista devices do not get a DID

INLINE RENAME (promptRenameDevice):
  - Clicking Ô£Ä replaces the name cell with a text <input> pre-filled with current name
  - Enter or blur ÔåÆ commits (if changed, calls checkForChanges() + renderManagerList())
  - Escape ÔåÆ cancels, re-renders without change
  - Uses `committed` flag to prevent double-commit on blur after Enter

INLINE DELETE (removeDeviceFromList / confirmRemoveDevice / cancelRemoveDevice):
  - State variable: pendingDeleteIndex (module-level, default -1)
  - Clicking Ô£ò sets pendingDeleteIndex = index and calls renderManagerList()
  - Affected row renders with red-tinted background + outline; delete cell shows
    Ô£ô (red confirm) and Ô£ò (cancel) buttons instead of the trash button
  - Ô£ô ÔåÆ confirmRemoveDevice(): splices list, resets index, checkForChanges(), re-renders
  - Ô£ò ÔåÆ cancelRemoveDevice(): resets index, re-renders
  - No window.confirm() used anywhere in delete flow

getExistingDevices():
  Reads current devices from sheet Row 1 (device name headers).
  Returns array of { name, type, isVisible, labels, did }.

getNonAristaList():
  Returns list of explicitly registered non-Arista device names.
  Stored in DocumentProperties under 'NON_ARISTA_DEVICES'.

SECTION 13: SCHEMA MANAGER
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

showDeviceDataUi() ÔåÆ 700x800 modeless dialog in 'schema' mode.

Schema is stored as a JSON array in DocumentProperties under 'SCHEMA_CONFIG_ARRAY'.
Falls back to DEFAULT_SCHEMA_ARRAY if missing/corrupt.

getSchemaConfig() / saveSchemaConfig(newArray) / resetSchemaToDefaults()
resetSchemaToDefaults(): confirm dialog clarifies "resets column definitions only ÔÇö sheet data not affected".

SCHEMA MODAL UI (schemaContainer, #schemaBody):
  Close button: btn-mono (matches all other modals).
  Add-row inputs: "Field key (e.g. rack_id)" + "Display label" placeholders.
  Footer (modal-actions, 3 footer-groups, ui-equal-size=128px):
    Left:   Reset Defaults (btn-danger)
    Center: "Apply Formatting" checkbox (chkApplyFormatting, title explains connection
            colors/conditional rules/MLAG borders/speed coding) + Check Sync (SVG
            magnifier) + Force Sync (SVG refresh)
